Spec Example 2.11. Mapping between Sequences

YAML

? - Detroit Tigers
  - Chicago cubs
:
  - 2001-07-23

? [ New York Yankees,
    Atlanta Braves ]
: [ 2001-07-02, 2001-08-12,
    2001-08-14 ]

+DOC
+MAP
+SEQ

-SEQ

=VAL :Atlanta Braves
-SEQ
+SEQ
=VAL :2001-07-02
=VAL :2001-08-12
=VAL :2001-08-14
-SEQ
-MAP
-DOC
-STR
